Special District: Emergency Meeting of Rickshaw Merchants 166

The Special District Office of the Rickshaw Industry Association, regarding the Municipal Council's recent announcement of the standards for new public rickshaws and the issuance of registration certificates to rickshaw owners, held a special emergency meeting of members yesterday at the Taihe Building Association Hall on Lloyd Road. More than 100 people attended, including Yin Zhiling, Gu Songmao, Bao Zhenhuang, and Zhu Hegao. The meeting was chaired by Liang Ruiting to discuss the Municipal Council's proposed standards for new public rickshaws. It was generally agreed that the standards were purely to cater to the curiosity of the nouveau riche and were not sturdy. Not only would it not improve public rickshaws or provide any benefit, but it would cause immense losses to the merchants. The Municipal Council's resolution on the public rickshaw design was to improve the design, making it sturdy, clean, and lightweight, and not to replace the currently licensed public rickshaws with completely new and different designs. It was resolved to maintain the current public rickshaws, improve their design, and negotiate with the Vehicle Affairs Committee. As for the Municipal Council's notice in the newspaper on the 9th, ordering all rickshaw owners to apply for a license and provide a guarantee to the association before the 14th, or else no license would be issued, it was generally agreed that the guarantee procedure should be presented to the Municipal Council to request an extension. Representatives were elected to meet in person to explain everything. The petition is recorded below:

Petition for an extension to the deadline for applying for a license: We read in the newspaper on June 9th about the Municipal Council's Notice No. 4477, which stated that rickshaw owners should obtain blank application forms for rickshaw owner certificates in writing from the Vehicle Affairs Committee office of the Municipal Council, fill them out according to the instructions, and submit them for review. The deadline is June 14th. If the application is deemed合格, the certificate will be issued, and the issuance date will be set. The certificate will be issued every two days starting from June 18th, with 100 certificates issued each time, until July 21st. After that date, if there is no certificate, the rickshaw will not be licensed. After reading this, we felt that the matter was of great importance. Therefore, on June 11th, we convened an emergency meeting of all members to discuss it. It was generally agreed that there are 10,000 rickshaws in the special district, and about 1,000 people operate them. The Municipal Council's method of only publishing the notice in the newspaper for one day and setting a deadline of only four days is extremely rushed. Rickshaw owners vary in intelligence, some read the newspaper and some do not. It is difficult to inform everyone in a short period of time. Moreover, some have other businesses and reside in other cities, so the news is delayed. It is even more difficult to complete the application and guarantee procedures in a hurry. Furthermore, the Municipal Council previously convened rickshaw owners to register, which took eight months and was repeatedly extended. The announcement has not yet been completed. Now, it is announced in the newspaper for only one day, without prior notice to all parties, ordering all rickshaw owners to apply for a license and provide a guarantee within four days, and to complete everything. Otherwise, no license will be issued, which is deeply shocking. We do not know what the Municipal Council's Vehicle Affairs Committee intends to achieve with this licensing method, and it is difficult to understand. However, rickshaw merchants, in order to maintain their capital and livelihood, cannot accept this method, which disregards the facts and the time. The resolution was passed to submit a petition to the Municipal Council to request an extension in order to avoid any omissions, and to elect representatives to meet in person to explain everything. The case is recorded accordingly, requesting the Municipal Council to review and approve the extension of the deadline for Notice No. 4477, in order to show consideration and facilitate the public. Respectfully submitted to the General Manager of the Municipal Council, Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Association Special District Office Standing Directors.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Writes to Public Utilities Bureau Regarding Improvement of Stamping Method on Barges 167

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, which read: "Respected Sirs, on the 10th of this month, we received a letter from the Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association, stating that after the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau inspects and measures Shanghai's barges, it stamps a hard-printed number on the rudder plate. The position is easy to step on, the lettering is shallow, and after being exposed to rain and sun, it will soon disappear. If the Shipping Office finds out, even if there is a license plate and a license, and proof of monthly payment, the boat owner will be accused of privately transferring the boat or forging the hard print. The boat is impounded and arbitrarily punished, even to the extent of several months of boat tax. Merchants request an investigation, or provide a guarantee, that if a barge with the same number is found, the guarantor will be responsible, but this is ignored. On May 12th, barges No. 12 to 26, No. 12649, No. 12504, and three boats were found by the Zhabei Shipping Office of the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau to have had their hard prints removed when the rudder plates were repaired. After the boat owners went to explain, No. 12526 was handled according to Article 4, Item 9 of the Shanghai Regulations for the Suppression of Cargo Ships, with a certificate from the shipyard and a guarantee, and was allowed to be reprinted. However, the other two boats were not allowed to be reprinted. This violates the same regulations, so why are the punishments different? This is incomprehensible. Although representatives have repeatedly petitioned the Public Utilities Bureau, the reply is always 'handled according to regulations.' Therefore, the merchant ships are now in a state of being unable to appeal. If this is not quickly improved, the suffering of the merchants will deepen day by day, and they may be forced to suspend operations. The first key point of improvement is to imitate the fire-branded prints used by the Customs and Municipal Council on seagoing ships and small vehicles, so that the lettering is clear and not easily removed, so that merchants are no longer wrongly accused. The second key point is to pay attention to whether the license plate and license of the barges whose hard prints have fallen off are consistent, and to check whether the boat tax paid to the Finance Bureau has been paid in full. In addition, if there is a certificate from the shipyard and a guarantor, they should be allowed to be reprinted immediately, without hindrance. As for the issue of grades, they are now suddenly different from the past. It is said that there are discounts of 20% and 10%, which is like buying and selling goods, allowing them to do whatever they want, which is not something that outsiders can know. Therefore, there is a real need to reform the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau's current method of suppressing cargo ships. Otherwise, it will not be possible to save the merchants from deep water and fire. The request is to have the conference forward a letter to the Public Utilities Bureau to fundamentally reform the management of ships in order to maintain commercial transportation.' We have reviewed Article 4, Item 8 of the Shanghai Provisional Penal Regulations for the Suppression of Cargo Ships, which states that if the steel seal number is blurry and unclear, a fine of 5 cents will be imposed. If the Shipping Office of the Public Utilities Bureau is immediately notified to reprint it, no additional fee will be charged. Furthermore, Item 9 of the same article states that if the original steel seal number position is removed due to repairs and is not reported for reprinting, a fine of 1 yuan will be imposed. Reprints of steel seals, as per Item 2 of the same article, privately transferring boats, is also only a fine of 1 yuan according to regulations. Privately removing the steel seal, according to Article 5, Item 3, is only a fine of 3 yuan. Why should there be so-called detention of boats and punishment, and even fines of several months of boat tax? We request that your bureau investigate this matter thoroughly to avoid excessive implementation. Regarding the two points of improvement requested by the association, the first point is to change the steel seal number to a fire-branded print, which is to make the lettering clearer and not easily removed. This would save your bureau the trouble of reprinting and save the merchants from wrongful fines, which would benefit both parties. If the steel seal is removed due to repairs and there is a certificate from the shipyard or a guarantee from the industry, they should be allowed to be reprinted according to regulations. With this appropriate certification from the authorities, it would not be based solely on one-sided statements, and the merchants would be spared the suspicion of transferring boats and falsifying seals, saving endless trouble. We respectfully request that you investigate and approve the implementation separately to achieve public friendship."

It has been learned that although the association's fundraising congress has concluded, the committee has resolved to set a three-week closing period, that is, until the end of this month. During this closing period, the closing will be handled on the one hand, and fundraising will continue on the other, so that as many Ningbo people in Shanghai as possible will join the association. The funds raised, in addition to using 30,000 yuan for two years of education expenses, will be used to repair the association's expenses. The association's standing committee member, the great architect Zhang Jiguang, has been appointed to handle the matter.

The Hangzhou Silk Group of the Shanghai Silk Industry Association (i.e., Qianjiang Guild Hall) on Ningbo Road in this port, in view of the lack of public libraries in Shanghai, in order to facilitate the spare time reading of the industry's shop assistants and improve their service efficiency, has established a Hangzhou Silk Industry Library. Guohua Bank Offers Factory Loans 173

The Guohua Bank on Beijing Road in this city, in order to assist the development of small industries run by Chinese people, held a factory loan program last month. It is reported that many people in the industrial sector went to apply for loans. Recently, the bank has also provided more convenient assistance to these factories, as factories purchase raw materials in cash, while the payments for the sale of finished products are mostly long-term and cannot be used immediately, which may affect their progress. For factories that sell raw materials to factories, or factories that sell finished products to wholesalers and meet the principles of factory loans, they can negotiate with the bank regarding the long-term payments receivable and use the method of exchanging notes and other procedures to borrow cash. This can be called a warm-hearted service to society and is an innovation in Shanghai's financial circles.

Later, the representative of the Municipal Party Department put forward three methods: (A) The membership fees and monthly fees owed by each member should be paid in full, and the legal resolution of last year's conference should not be overturned. (B) If any member believes that there are discrepancies in the association's income and expenditure accounts, they may publicly elect several auditors to review the accounts. (C) In the future, if the association's constitution is to be amended regarding membership fees, it must be proposed at today's conference. Subsequently, the members who owed membership fees could not comply with the opinions of the representative of the Municipal Party Department, so the meeting ended without a result. The association has now reported the progress of the meeting to the superior authorities.

The Flower and Tree Industry Association, because the flower shop business has plummeted and is difficult to maintain, and the shops are asking for rent reductions, a meeting of flower shop representatives was specially convened yesterday to establish a rent reduction branch. More than 30 flower shop representatives and 9 executive committee members attended. Huang Yueyuan chaired the meeting and performed the ceremony. First, Hong Songjiong, a member of the committee, reported on the association's participation in the work of the Promotion Association. Next, Mr. Qiu Liangyu, a representative of the Promotion Association, gave guidance on the procedures and implementation methods for requesting rent reduction. Then, the discussion began and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The Flower and Tree Industry Branch of the Rent Reduction Promotion Association will be established immediately, with the original executive committee members serving as members of the Rent Reduction Branch. (2) In accordance with the notice of the Promotion Association, the period from the 11th to the 20th of this month will be the general mobilization date, and the payment of rent will be suspended uniformly. (3) Before the rent reduction is resolved, the rent will be stored in the bank at the original rent amount. (4) The flower shops proposed that flower vendors have recently been blocking customers and hawking flowers in front of the flower shops, which is detrimental to the shop's business. They requested that measures be taken to ban this. It was resolved to send personnel to the market first to use the New Life Movement to persuade flower vendors not to hawk in front of flower shops, but to sell ten storefronts away from flower shops, and not to surround pedestrians on the road and compete to sell, obstructing traffic. The above guidance method will be notified to each flower shop, which will each be guided in front of their stores. The deadline is from the 15th to the 30th. After the deadline, the resolutions will be enforced. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Eye specialist Tong Shaofu is a direct descendant of ten generations of old eye doctors from Liyang. His family has deep roots in the field, and he has inherited ancestral secret methods. Having served his hometown for many years, he has long been admired by the local people. In 1926, he founded the Tong Bao Mu Tang Eye Clinic in Wuxi. In the nine years since then, countless people have had their eyesight restored. People from several counties, including Liyang, Yixing, Jintan, Changzhou, Jiangyin, and Wuxi, all know of him. For example, the daughter of Mr. Chen Youshen, the section chief of the Jinpu Railway, lost her eyesight in her right eye for eight years after an illness. After careful diagnosis and treatment by Dr. Tong, she fully recovered in a few months. He has now come to Shanghai at the invitation of relatives and friends in the area to open a clinic at No. 17 Yongxiang Lane, Datong Road, Zhabei. He has already cured many eye diseases and is truly a skilled ophthalmologist.

Reading Q&A: On Plagiarism 丨 Reply to Mr. Xu Ke 丨 182

The "Free Talk" section of this newspaper once published an article by Maxim Gorky titled "What Books Should Children Read?", which included the following passage:

"Science and inventions should not be written as a ready-made account of discoveries and inventions, but as a battlefield of human struggle against material obstacles and traditional ideas. The compilers of such books should be well-researched scientists, not book-compiling craftsmen who copy from here and there; only through the cooperation of true scientists and talented writers can we engage in publishing books that disseminate scientific knowledge with artistic skill."

After reading this passage, Mr. Xu Ke raised the following two questions for us:

(1) Any discipline must have related subjects. For example, when a physiologist writes about physiology, he inevitably has to refer to anatomy. How can he avoid the suspicion of copying from here and there?

(2) What is the difference between compiling a popular version of a famous work and copying from here and there?

We accept Mr. Xu's questions and offer some correct interpretations of plagiarism, because this is helpful for readers in distinguishing the quality of a book, and even when compiling a work.

Based on the questions raised by Mr. Xu, we feel that Mr. Xu not only does not fully understand Gorky's passage, but also seems to not fully understand the meaning of the word "plagiarism."

Plagiarism refers to an author taking someone else's article and presenting it as his own. Plagiarism is different from citation. Citation is the open use of someone else's words to prove one's own argument, while plagiarism is ambiguous in the author's attitude. He does not indicate the author and source of the original text, and his own writing does not have a fixed point of view, but only uses phrases that others are accustomed to using as embellishment. If a physiologist wants to use anatomy when writing about physiology, then he should not hesitate to indicate the source of the original text, and especially should ensure that the cited sentences are not just filler, but are part of the entire system of his own article, becoming something that complements his own views, or precisely what he wants to write. In this way, it is clearly not plagiarism but citation. All "copycats" can be called "petty thieves." They hold the view that "whatever is in hand is wealth." Randomly stealing may sometimes lead to one or two real treasures, but sometimes they may also "mistake dog poop for treasure." Although they themselves do not have the ability to distinguish wealth, they undoubtedly rely on "theft" to survive. The writers who took the imperial examinations in the past were masters of this trick. I remember a joke that describes the general "copycat." Before entering the examination hall, the candidate stuffed many prepared "crib sheets" written in tiny characters into the small brush handle. When the examination question was released, he took out his treasures from the brush handle. It just so happened that there was an article among the treasures that was exactly on the topic. He copied it out with satisfaction, naturally believing that he would undoubtedly "pass with honors." Who knew that fate was perverse. The text on the crib sheet was abbreviated. Our copycat mistakenly wrote the first two words of the "introduction" (昔賢, "wise men," with 賢 abbreviated as 　) as "the twenty-first day ascends to heaven" (廿一日上天). As a result, the examiner picked up a vermilion pen before even reading the entire article and wrote six large characters: "Dare not detain the immortal." And so, a red hat was lightly sent away. This joke is the most vivid description of the ignorance of "copycats."

However, the "copying from here and there" in Gorky's passage does not refer to such shallow plagiarism, but is a further statement.

Gorky meant that to write scientific truths into children's reading material, simply copying from here and there and bringing out some scientific terms or principles verbatim is unsuccessful. The scientific language should be dissolved under one's own pen and become artistic language. Therefore, the cooperation of qualified scientists and outstanding writers is essential. Here, the so-called plagiarism is not only about understanding the problem, but also about dissolving the problem, not only about the size of the clippings, but also about the use of words. This is precisely aimed at the popular culture movement.

Using Gorky's words to explain the second question raised by Mr. Xu, we can say this:

To adapt world famous works into popular versions, not only must the language be popularized, but also the content must be popularized. The compiler must not distort the original work's views, but also cannot just circle within the original work's framework. For example, when compiling a popular version of a literary masterpiece, you cannot just excerpt passages from the original work and call it a day. You must write it in your own most popular language so that people see a completely new face. Otherwise, although it is called popular, it is not popular at all, and can only be regarded as "plagiarism." It is even more necessary to do this when adapting scientific masterpieces. Therefore, adaptation is not "plagiarism." A reviser who fails to dissolve the original work and only spits it out verbatim, without achieving the goal of popularization, is guilty of "plagiarism."

We hope that all those involved in the popular culture movement should pay attention to Gorky's passage.

Attention to Practice and Guidance in Tennis 192

Must Study Training Methods

The Fen Bookstore at 39 Father Lao Road in the French Concession, Shanghai, has recently released expert masterpieces on tennis, from the shallow to the deep, from training to refining and achieving success and secrets. No book is missing, no book is not refined. The contents of each book are detailed as follows: (1) "Tennis Training Method" is written by tennis veteran Madetai. The whole book is divided into ten chapters, and each chapter is further divided into small sections. It gives detailed descriptions and practical guidance on how to study tennis, various methods of holding the racket and hitting the ball, as well as single and double competition methods, key points during the competition, attitudes, key points during the training of players, on-the-spot policies, and winning secrets. It also includes ten copperplate illustrations of Zheng Zhaojia's performance postures, so that readers can follow the pictures and find their way without a teacher. This is a must-read book for beginners in tennis. The price per copy is 50 cents. (2) "Tennis Secrets" was originally written by Ms. Bai Lang, the American women's tennis singles and doubles champion, and translated by Wu Bangwei, the principal of the Provincial Sports Field. The whole book is divided into twenty-two chapters, and each chapter is further divided into sections. The content includes secrets of holding the racket, essentials of hitting the ball, footwork, movements, counterattacks, rebounds, timing of hitting the ball, spin and chop, the center of gravity and movement of serving, smash, hitting high balls, drawing side balls, on-the-spot essentials, jumping strikes, foot position and angle changes, doubles strategy, singles strategy, competition and psychology, racket selection, and model tennis players. It thoroughly explores and carefully describes everything, and includes many photos of active postures for reference. This is a must-read for those who are doing in-depth research on tennis and who are well-trained in tennis and seeking further study. The price per copy is 70 cents. (3) "Tilden's Tennis Techniques" was originally written by Boris, a famous American tennis coach, and translated by Ruan Weicun, a sports writer. The whole book is divided into ten chapters. The content includes a basic understanding of tennis and skills, hand-holding the racket and foot movements, drawing the ball, serving, interception, smash, high ball, cross-cut low interception, and increasing the position on the field. It gives concise and detailed descriptions and separate guidance. This is a special book for studying Tilden's tennis techniques. The techniques are deeper, and those who are practicing tennis should also purchase it for reference. The price per copy is 50 cents. (4) "Winning Secrets in the World of Tennis" was written by Madame Madi, the third tennis master. The content is the self-description of the experience, technology, and success of three experts. 1. The Tennis Championship, 2. Where are the mistakes in the game, 3. How to create a tennis player. This book is full of carefully researched experience theory, and is the only masterpiece that tennis players must read before the game. The price per copy is 45 cents. (5) "Lin Baohua's Success Story in Tennis" was compiled by Shen Bao sports reporter Jiang Huaiqing. The whole book is divided into seventeen chapters. The content includes Lin's family, the beginning of playing ball and becoming famous, as well as the 8th Far Eastern Games, the Davis Cup, the Michigan State and New Jersey State Championships, the runner-up of the American Western Tennis Tournament, the runner-up of the Misha State, defeating the Honolulu Championship Carnival, the National Divisional Tennis Tournament, a new era in the Shanghai tennis world, the results of the competition, and the most memorable words. It also includes many valuable photos. All those who love tennis and admire Lin should refer to this book. The price per copy is 30 cents. (6) "Qiu Juhai's Success Story in Tennis" was compiled by Shenqing sports reporter Jiang Huaiqing. The whole book is divided into ten chapters. The content includes Mr. Qi's experience, ball skills, temperament, appearance in Huiborden, the achievements in the Far Eastern Games, dealing with world famous players, three battles with Lin Baohua, the honor of the Shanghai International Championship, the most glorious record of battle, Qiu's self-described biography, the future of the Chinese tennis world, etc. It also includes many valuable photos. All those who love tennis and admire Qiu's ball skills should also have this book. The price per copy is 30 cents. The above six types are all famous works in the current tennis world, and are must-reads for those in the general tennis world. They are all sold at a 10% discount during this tennis season, which is a very good opportunity to purchase them. In addition, the "Tennis Rules" booklet costs 8 cents. All of these books are also sold at the same price at the storefront of the bureau at 277 Sima Road.

Jiangsu Revises National Language Teaching Schedule Committee Meeting 200

Over 200 Model Essays Selected for Junior High School

Arranging Order Based on Difficulty of Writing

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Committee for Revising the National Language Teaching Schedule held its fifth meeting at 9:00 AM on the 9th in the Education Department's conference room. Attendees included Wu Qining, Xu Shengyue, Li Dajiu, Hong Beiping, Zhang Xuhou, Wang Delin, and Xiang Shaoxuan, with Xiang Shaoxuan presiding. The meeting followed the usual procedure. A. Report Items. B. Resolutions. (1) From the already compiled list of model essays for junior high school, those that receive majority approval will be selected first. Notes should be added below, indicating whether they should be taught in senior high school, in which grade of junior high school, whether they should be listed alongside a certain essay, or attached after a certain essay. As a result, 104 essays were selected, and each committee member will be responsible for reviewing, signing and adding comments, and estimating the number of words for planning purposes. (2) Committee members Wang Delin and Hong Beiping were assigned to draft a system of arrangement, using the difficulty of writing as the general principle. Besides this, some flexibility is allowed. The weight of the first three semesters should be slightly heavier, in order to free up time to read Mencius. As for the distribution of vernacular texts, it should also be slightly more in the first semester, decreasing gradually thereafter. (3) All senior high school model essays selected by the committee members will be submitted to Committee Member Wang Delin for compilation. Committee Members Zhang Xuhou, Xu Shengyue, and Wu Qining will, according to the standards promulgated by the Ministry, draft a system of arrangement for each academic year, with literary style as the framework for the first academic year, the origin and development of literature as the framework for the second academic year, and academic thought as the framework for the third academic year. The materials compiled by Committee Member Wang Delin should be sent to Committee Members Zhang, Xu, and Wu as soon as possible to facilitate their drafting. The errors in punctuation and correction of typos in the model essays reviewed by the committee members should indicate which books they are based on for verification. Regarding annotation, each committee member should draft annotation examples separately and submit them for discussion at the meeting. The sixth meeting is scheduled to be held at 9:00 AM on June 16th.

Regarding the directors or supervisors of physical education who manage physical education, in order to promote national physical education, a special order is issued to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to quickly establish it.

Zhejiang Provincial Education Department Holds Middle School Moral Education Conference 209

Group Discussions on Proposals and Invitations to Famous People to Give Lectures

The Zhejiang Provincial Education Department held the opening ceremony of the provincial middle school moral education conference at 9:00 AM on the 11th. Forty-five people attended, including principals and moral education directors of various public middle schools. First, Department Director Ye Suzhong gave an opening speech, stating that the establishment of the class teacher system in Zhejiang Province in 1933 was intended to lay the foundation for the unification of teaching and discipline, and that the common life of teachers and students is the main method for implementing the unification of teaching and discipline. It is hoped that this will continue to be promoted in the future. The provincial principals' meeting in the previous semester made important decisions on moral education facilities, such as the youth ideological guidance program. It is hoped that this moral education conference will produce more concrete results. The main topics to be discussed are the temporary standards for moral education in middle schools in the province, the temporary examination methods for adopting grades, the national defense education program, and other guidance plans in various aspects such as labor, etiquette, autonomy, using domestic goods, extracurricular reading, and health education. Next, representatives from the provincial party headquarters, Fang Ru, and the provincial government, Zhang Heng, delivered speeches. Subsequently, Lu Dianyang and Wang Junsheng gave speeches. Then, the first general meeting was continued, dividing into four groups. The first group was for rules and regulations, the second group was for life guidance, the third group was for health and hygiene, and the fourth group was for magazines. Each person identified one or two groups. A lecture meeting was held at 1:30 PM, with Zhuang Zexuan of Zhejiang University lecturing on youth training in England, Germany, and Italy. At 3:00 PM, each group held a review meeting separately. The second general meeting is scheduled to continue at 8:00 AM today.

Municipal Elementary School Representatives Visit the Director of the Education Bureau 210

Funding for May and June Will Be Issued Before the Holiday

Study of Educational Matters to Be Determined After Approval by the Municipal Government

(Shanghai) The municipal school funding for this semester has been in arrears for two months, making it difficult for the schools to maintain operations. Therefore, representatives were dispatched to the Education Bureau and the Municipal Government to petition the day before yesterday. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. It was heard yesterday that five representatives, Qian Cijiu, Li Zhanren, Yu Shumin, Xu Yuchang, and Yang Songyu, visited Director Pan to discuss the funding for May and June and the assignment of municipal school teachers and staff to study education at home and abroad. Director Pan gave detailed answers, stating that the bureau is paying great attention to the lives of teachers and staff, and will do its best to raise funds for May and June, which will be issued before the holiday. He asked all teachers and staff to serve with peace of mind in order to focus on the students' studies. He also expressed his support for the assignment of teachers and staff to study education at home and abroad, and decided to include the study expenses in next year's budget, but it must be approved by the Municipal Government before a method can be determined. The representatives considered it satisfactory and bid farewell and returned.

Shanghai One-Man Show Research Association Established Yesterday 213

Over 80 Members from the City Attended

Liu Chunshan and Others Elected as Directors and Supervisors

The preparation for the organization of the Shanghai One-Man Show Performers Research Association has been completed. The inaugural meeting was held yesterday morning at 10:00 AM in the lecture hall of the Municipal Education Center. The details are as follows:

The attending members included Liu Chunshan, Jiang Xiaoxiao, Pei Yanghua, Zhu Xiangfei, Liu Kuaile, Lü Xiaofeng, Tang Xiaofei, Xiao Xixi, He Shuangdai, Xu Gudong, Deng Xiaoling, Zhongxin Xiao, Wu Youhen, Xue Lingqiao, Wu Xiuzhen, Shen Xiuqin, Sheng Daidai, Xia Xiuzhen, Xiao Xiuying, Zhao Xixi, Chen Haxiao, Cheng Xiaoting, Bai Yuquan, Tang Tianxiao, and others, totaling over 80 people. Zhu Jiarang, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yuan Zengyu and Ding Shoutang, representatives of the Municipal Education Bureau, and Lei Kenan, representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, attended to provide guidance.

Meeting Proceedings: The meeting commenced at 10:00 AM, and Liu Chunshan, Pei Yanghua, Zhu Xiangfei, Zhongxin Xiao, and Tang Xiaofei were jointly elected as the presidium. After the formalities, Liu Chunshan reported on the preparations and the significance of the meeting. Subsequently, Zhu Jiarang, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Yuan Zengyu, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, and Lei Kenan, representative of the Social Affairs Bureau, delivered speeches. The proposals were then discussed, and the directors and supervisors were elected before adjourning.

Discussion of Proposals: (1) Proposal on Unifying the Name of One-Man Shows: It was resolved that the name "One-Man Show" should be used uniformly for the table used by each performer during performances. (2) Proposal on Determining Membership Fees: It was resolved that each member should pay one yuan per month, with unemployed members being exempt. (3) Proposal on Holding Regular Variety Shows to Raise Funds: It was resolved that two shows should be held each year, with the dates to be determined by the board of directors. (4) Proposal on Specifying the Date of the Annual General Meeting: It was resolved that the meeting should be held on September 7th. (5) Proposal on Relieving Unemployed, Elderly, and Sick Colleagues: It was resolved to hand it over to the board of directors for detailed planning. (6) Proposal on Organizing a Play Material Review Committee: It was resolved to hand it over to the board of directors for handling. (7) Proposal on Applying to the Competent Authorities for the Issuance of Personal Registration Certificates to Colleagues: It was resolved to approve it. (8) Proposal on Holding a New Life Movement Week: It was resolved to approve it, and the board of directors will determine the method, with colleagues uniformly promoting the New Life Movement during performances. The remaining proposals were omitted.

Election Results: Liu Chunshan, Pei Yanghua, Fan Haha, Jiang Xiaoxiao, Bao Lele, Sheng Daidai, and Zhao Xixi were elected as directors. Jiang Youkui, He Shuangdai, and Cheng Xiaoting were elected as alternate directors. Zhu Xiangfei, Lu Xixi, and Lü Xiaofeng were elected as supervisors. Liu Kuaile and Zhongxin Xiao were elected as alternate supervisors.

Dr. Wu Bizhang Studies Stomach Diseases 216

Wu Bizhang, Ph.D. in Surgical Philosophy from Columbia University, is the first person in our country to obtain this degree in the United States. After returning to China this year, Dr. Wu was hired by the Lester Institute of Medical Research in Shanghai, where he is studying the causes and treatment of stomach diseases. Mr. Wu initially studied at St. John's University in Shanghai and studied medicine in the United States for nine years, obtaining a Doctor of Medicine degree from the University of Virginia, a Master of Surgery degree from the University of Minnesota, and a Doctor of Surgical Philosophy degree from Columbia University.

IP> Photo of Dr. Wu Bizhang

Great China University Establishes an Education Museum 217

Since its establishment, Great China University has developed rapidly, earning a distinguished reputation. The number of students coming from afar has been increasing daily. The university's College of Education and Teacher Training Department are places for researching educational academics and training teachers, and have made great progress in recent years. The number of students has increased to more than 500. The professors are all talented individuals of the time. To facilitate students' exploration of education, an Educational Research Room has been established outside the university library. The collected educational reference books include more than 200 kinds of Chinese educational gazettes and magazines, more than 300 kinds of general gazettes and magazines, and more than 1,000 books on education, totaling more than 50,000 volumes. There are also about 1,000 Western books, including about 600 books on education, mostly works on the history of education and educational theories. There are about 5,000 copies of English educational magazines and pamphlets, with various items available. In addition, there are newspaper clippings from the Republic of China's 13th year to the present. Educational and socio-economic data related to education from more than a dozen famous domestic newspapers have been clipped onto large cards, totaling about 100,000 sheets. The wealth of collections is second to none among domestic universities. Recently, the university is planning to establish an Educational Research Institute and intends to expand the existing Educational Research Room into an Education Museum. The university affairs meeting has passed the resolution and is about to begin. It is heard that the organization of the museum will consist of three departments: research, compilation, and exhibition. The research department will establish various research rooms according to the research needs of the College of Education and the Teacher Training Department, collect reference materials on education, and set up various instruments. The compilation department will have (1) a clipping room, clipping materials from various newspapers, pasting them on cards, classifying and compiling them for reference; and (2) an index room, compiling indexes of educational papers published in various publications as tools for research. (According to this semester's work, it has already begun, and it is expected that 150,000 cards can be made.) The exhibition department will have four rooms: (1) a toy room, displaying various toys with educational significance; (2) an achievement room, displaying various achievements in educational administration, school education, and social education. The achievements of children's education are also attached here; (3) a teaching aid room, displaying educational specimens, models, health inspection equipment, and various educational tools; (4) a school equipment room, displaying various school-style equipment and physical education equipment, etc. Regarding the above equipment, in addition to transferring or supplementing the university's existing equipment, achievements, toys, etc. will be solicited from all parties at the university's tenth anniversary conference. As for school equipment and education, in addition to manufacturing a part by the students, the rest is planned to be solicited for long-term display, referring to the method of the Educational Reporting Bureau of the Prussian State of Germany, for exhibition and research. The required expenses are about 10,000 yuan for building the museum and about 2,000 yuan for equipment. Detailed budget is still being calculated. According to our country's educational research, the cause is still in its early stages. The special establishment of the Education Museum is still an initiative. Now, the university is dedicated to this, opening a new era in the history of education in our country.

Chongde Girls' Middle School Holds Concert 218

The private Chongde Girls' Middle School in this city usually pays great attention to extracurricular activities. Many students participate in activities such as the Literary Society, the Music Society, and the Speech Society. The Music Society has achieved the best results, with Li Xianmin, a famous pianist in Shanghai, serving as a professor. Last winter, the Music Society hosted a concert, which received good reviews from Chinese and foreign newspapers and experts. The school is scheduled to hold a student concert at 3:00 PM on the 16th of this month in the school auditorium. There are more than 30 programs, including Beethoven's Model Great Music, Chopin's Preludes, Svendsen's Impromptu, and works by the world-renowned musical composer Derz, who is currently traveling in China, and Ms. Li, which were performed in the Great Light Building. In addition, performances by children with artistic talent aged six or seven are rare.

Jinan Drama Club's Performance Today

The performances were all extremely wonderful.

Furthermore, Jinan University has an organization called the "Jinan Drama Club." The "January 28th Incident" led to its suspension. This semester, former members and faculty and students who love drama have been working on its revival to restore its former glory. They are scheduled to hold their first performance at 8:00 PM on the 13th of this month in the university auditorium. The program includes "The Tide," "Opposing Fishing Tax," and "She Might Not Agree" (one-act play), directed by Zuo Ming, Xu Suling, Gu Zhongyi, and Wang Shaoqing, and starring Jin Guangmei, Shu Yan, Liang Tianzhen, and others. Furthermore, Bao Shi, Wu Tie, and Gong Erjun from the Fudan Drama Club will be guest performers. Tickets are priced at two and four dimes, respectively, and are sold by the Modern Bookstore and the New China Bookstore. After the show, public buses will be available to return to Shanghai.

China Child Education Society Japanese Study Notes (7) 221

— Zhou Shang

The general education in Kobe has already been briefly described in the previous section. Now, I will record my observations from visiting various schools in the city, using the strengths of each school as a theme to inform the nation.

As I have repeatedly stated, the first school we visited was the Kobe Municipal Kitano Elementary School, on the morning of April 4th at 8:00 AM. We were guided by Shi Yunfeng, a classmate from Waseda University, and Dong Gongxu, the principal of the Kobe-Osaka Chinese Public School. Upon arrival, we saw the Chinese and Japanese flags flying side-by-side at the school gate, waving in the wind. All the faculty members stood beside the gate, bowing respectfully to welcome us into the auditorium. We were treated to a generous offering of tea and snacks. The female teachers brewed fragrant tea and served pastries, meticulously attentive to avoid any discourtesy. It is said that Japanese elementary schools have very few janitors; all miscellaneous tasks are handled by the faculty. Even taking tea and cleaning napkins, they did everything themselves. The school principal, Iwuo Tabuchi, is 43 years old and the youngest principal in Kobe. The citizens often use this as a topic of conversation. On that day, he had gone to Tokyo to attend the "National Elementary School Teachers' Development Association" and had not yet returned. The so-called Elementary School Teachers' Development Association is a revitalization association for elementary school teachers, the largest gathering in the Japanese education sector in recent years. Its purpose is to commemorate the birth of the crown prince and awaken 300,000 elementary school teachers to engage in the positive guidance of children and young people's thoughts. The meeting was held in Tokyo on April 1st. Emperor Showa attended and delivered an instruction, including an imperial edict stating:

"To invigorate national morality and lead to the prosperity of the nation, the foundation lies in elementary school education. Those in charge should strive diligently day and night." This kind of imperial edict is like the imperial decrees of our country in the past. It is the new goal of Japanese education, restoring the education goals of cultivating local customs and shaping character from that time. This covers the tenets of Confucianism and the key points of the New Life Movement, so I am not afraid of being tedious and elaborate on it.

The acting principal was Kiyokazu Wakitani, the school's guidance counselor. His welcoming speech was printed beforehand and distributed to us. After the greetings, we observed the physical exercises of the sixth-grade students. Male and female students were taught separately by male and female teachers at the same time and place. Each student's muscles were developed, their posture was graceful, and their spirit was full of energy. The observers were amazed. Despite the cold weather, they wore only a thermal shirt on their upper bodies and short pants on their lower bodies, with bare legs and feet. After only a moment of practice, each of them was dripping with sweat. The teachers' commands were exceptionally loud. Their brave and progressive state was like facing a great enemy. They first practiced preparatory exercises, individual flexibility exercises, rib cage exercises, vaulting horse exercises, and finally abdominal exercises, handstand exercises, and breathing exercises. What we noted here was: (1) every child has an opportunity to exercise, (2) every child's performance is above the standard level, (3) every child can develop their inherent nature, (4) various exercises emphasize hard training for boys and graceful aesthetics for girls, (5) physical education teachers are also homeroom teachers. I once heard a Japanese representative report at the World Health Education Conference that his country's physical education focuses on both the physical and spiritual aspects. The former is about the development of physique, and the latter is about the cultivation of temperament. The Ministry of Education established a physical education department in 1921, specializing in supervising physical training inside and outside schools. Even in remote rural areas, there are experts to guide physical education research associations. Physical education league associations were established ten years ago to engage in activities. There are countless physical education publications. It is not an exaggeration to call Japan a physical education nation. However, whether the object of their physical training is for the sake of physical education or for some other purpose is something that puzzles me.

Kobe is known for physical education in Japan, and Kitano is famous for physical education in Kobe. The acting principal, Wakitani, is a well-known figure in Japanese elementary school physical education. He studied in Switzerland for several years, specializing in Swiss gymnastics, and has written extensively. After returning to Japan, he continued to serve in elementary schools. He is sincere and kind, and every night he came to the hostel to talk and gave the reporter many books on health education. The reporter inquired about the physical education teaching materials of various schools. He said that the physical education teaching materials for Kobe elementary schools are unified throughout the city. Every school has morning assemblies where all teachers and students attend to exercise their bodies. Each day, sports meetings are held, and grand mass exercises take place daily. In addition to gymnastics, there are martial arts such as kendo, judo, and boxing. There is a reason for the health of the people of this nation.

Physical education is to a country what essence is to the human body. Looking broadly at China and foreign countries, there has never been a person without essence who is healthy, and even more so, there has never been a country without proper education that is strong. Physical education is probably a good medicine for curing the weakness of our nation. There are many Japanese elementary schools in Shanghai. All our elementary school teachers, at least principals and physical education teachers, should go to observe their physical education and think about how to thoroughly reform it. The wind and rain are dark, and the cock crows endlessly. The idea of holding a weapon to defend the country is widespread, awaiting the rise of physical education. The reporter is willing to offer enthusiasm, hoping that the people of the country will value physical education.

After the gymnastics class, we observed the preparation rooms for each subject. The so-called preparation room is a room that provides all the materials needed for teaching. For example, the geography preparation room has all the maps, models, products, instruments, etc., gathered in the room for teachers to use and students to practice. The same goes for each subject. We went to the sewing room and saw the students busy cutting and sewing. Girls can choose this course starting from the fifth grade. When starting to learn to use sewing machines, they first use paper to practice stepping on straight lines, then use an iron to smooth them. There are about a dozen sewing machines. Younger students can use hand-cranked machines.

After the observation, the school students performed various children's songs and dances such as the Moon Viewing Night Ball, the Feudal Lords, the Army Game, the Knights, the Air Fleet, the Hengjie, and the Prince. The content is all militarized, reflecting nothing but the samurai spirit of the Yamato people.

The school covers an area of 1,579 square meters, with 3,833 square meters of open space. The construction cost a total of 85,394 yen. The architectural style is modern reinforced concrete, three stories. Yet, they are still not satisfied and complain about the simplicity of the school building. It is common to see elementary school buildings in Japan costing over two million yen.

Records of Fragrant Incense 222

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

But the people in front were tired enough, they were not allowed to walk backwards; they had to face forward like the people behind, and then bend their arms backwards to hold the edges of the trays, walking slowly. Imagine: Each tray held three dragon robes, each tray carried by two eunuchs, so how long would this line be when the Empress Dowager wanted to inspect her clothes?

Since the Empress Dowager owned such a huge amount of clothing, she could of course change them at any time. But because their number was so excessive, even if she changed twice or three times a day, many clothes would never be worn; although their material was equally beautiful and their embroidery was equally exquisite, the Empress Dowager simply did not think of them for a while, and they had to be relegated to the cold palace! Some of them were emotional and commemorative, which were the clothes she wore when she first entered the palace as a noble concubine decades ago. Because of this commemorative relationship, although she never wore them again, she often had the eunuchs bring them out to play with, seemingly savoring them. At this time, I could often infer her inner feelings from her facial expressions. She was trying her best to recall her past beauty and many beautiful scenes and good times, and she also wanted to get some youthful joy from her illusions. So she always thought very intently, even for several minutes; when she was thinking intently, no one was allowed to speak to her, so as not to interrupt her thoughts. Even if I had something to report to her, 丨now that I think about it, I was very bold at that time, often ignoring how intently she was thinking, I still spoke as usual.丨She would never pay attention to me.

(Five or Six)

Such Paradise 223

— Shijiu

Whenever Suzhou and Hangzhou are mentioned, everyone seems to hold an envious feeling, thinking that the people living there must have a comfortable life like living in paradise, and they can eat without worrying. That's right, Suzhou and Hangzhou have roads, banks, large hotels, dazzling neon lights, and the temptation of meat, the aroma of wine, etc.: so eating is good, living is good, wearing is good. In short, if a place doesn't have these, then it doesn't deserve to be called "paradise," then the title of paradise, Suzhou and Hangzhou can indeed be worthy of it, and the people living there are also worthy of pride.

I don't know what the situation is in Suzhou; now let's talk about Hangzhou.

A friend told me that he was returning from somewhere, a few steps away from his house, and was stopped by a rickshaw puller. He said sadly, "Sir, please take my rickshaw. From eight in the morning until almost noon now, I haven't found a single customer!" After saying that, the rickshaw puller was already in tears.

Pork is extremely cheap, one dollar can buy six catties! (market scale) Everyone is surprised, so it's a bargain, it seems that everyone can feast on it. However, whenever I walk past the butcher shop in the afternoon, I often see large pieces hanging on iron hooks, covered with white cloth, and the people in the shop often use brooms dipped in water to sprinkle on the meat.

From Yangbatou to Baoyoufang, what you see are phrases such as "regardless of cost," "add one and give five," "closing down sale," "special sacrifice," "this store always adheres to the principle of small profits"; what you hear are military music and ten-beat gongs and drums playing dirges wildly, with a very weeping and complaining tone. The colorful arches across the street, although still standing upright, smile bitterly at people, but who goes to squint at them!

If there are such scenes in paradise, then Hangzhou is truly enviable, but I don't know about Suzhou.

(Editor's note: Suzhou is also like this. Alas, paradise!)

Standard of Living 224

— Weijing

Thirty years ago, someone earning one hundred yuan a year was already a top scholar, not to mention when it came to marriage, red horoscopes, whatever amount was asked, was given. Even when strolling leisurely on the street, the elders in the village would have to treat them with respect and courtesy, flattering them. In fact, at that time, one yuan could only be exchanged for eight hundred Kangxi large white coins. One hundred yuan a year, exchanged for only eighty thousand large coins.

Things are not right this year, someone earning one hundred yuan a month, although one yuan can be exchanged for three hundred and thirty copper coins, in reality, one hundred yuan is worth three hundred and thirty thousand "Kong Brothers," but in the eyes of most people, although it is not said to be enough to avoid begging, it is probably not seen as very desirable.

Only a difference of thirty years before and after, the difference in the standard of living has undeniably undergone a huge change. Look, one Kangxi large white coin from the past is worth so much more than a copper coin this year.

The current dollar price is always above three thousand. I have an absurd fantasy, if a copper coin now was really worth ten Kangxi large white coins from thirty years ago, then needless to say, there would never be traces of bandits and beggars in this world.

But, at present, the value of a copper coin is only worth a copper coin. I fear that thirty years from now, a double dime silver coin will probably not be worth the value of a copper coin today. By then, not to mention someone earning one hundred yuan a month not being able to survive, even someone earning one hundred yuan a day might have some difficulty.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 225

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty

Burying Heads to Defend the Homeland, Watching the Weeping Geese

A Bullet Pierces a Strong Arm, Blood Stains a Lonely City

Unable to find an envelope, he rummaged through the stationery box for a long time and found a sheet of form paper, which he folded into the shape of an envelope, wrapped the letter, wrote the recipient's name and address, and then quietly walked out. He found an acquaintance among the common people, held his hand, and said in a low voice: "Old fellow, I have something I want to ask you to do." As he said this, he took out a silver dollar from his pocket and stuffed it into his hand. The old fellow took the money, stared with wide eyes, not knowing how to answer. Ziqiang then stuffed the letter into his hand and said with a wry smile: "This is a letter to my family. Please do me a favor and take it to a town, buy some stamps, and mail it for me." The old fellow said: "Officer, I'll take it for you, buying some stamps won't cost that much money." Ziqiang said: "We're going to close the doors and fight here, money is useless. You're a refugee, carrying a dollar with you, it's a good thing, take it. As long as you're willing to take it there sooner or later, I'll be grateful beyond measure." The old fellow said: "Officer, everyone needs help sometimes, I'll definitely deliver it, you can rest assured." Ziqiang clasped his fists, bowed to him twice, and then turned and left. In this way, he seemed to have gained great comfort, as if a lump was stuck in his chest, and he had now taken it out. Whenever soldiers miss their families, they have no other way to relieve this pain, only two ways to seek comfort. One is to receive a letter from home, and the other is to write a letter to home. But receiving a letter from home is not an easy thing, almost never happening. So when Ziqiang wrote the words on the letter, it was as if he was talking to his family. Sending the letter out was like his family hearing him. On the last day of preserved communication, he had to send this letter to his family, and his heart was very happy. With no more worries, he started working according to the battalion commander's orders. (◯ Seven)

Love Crimes 226

— Ziwei

Plato said: "A woman's whole life is enveloped in love." This statement is somewhat overly focused on the female side. In fact, whether male or female, when the flame of youth burns most fiercely, they need the comfort of love.

Speaking of love, some people see it as too mysterious, even taking it as an ultimate thing, worshiping it like an idol foolishly, humiliating themselves in a crazy manner, and burying their happiness and lives in this infatuated soil. That piece of their true, ardent love is sure to gain the sympathy and pity of the general public.

However, there are other people with opposite personalities, whose attitude is frivolous and unfaithful. Their devotion to love fails to last and be dedicated. They often use love as a means of deception, fooling and ruining the other party. Like these people, they are all prisoners waiting for trial before the seat of the god of love.

It is said that in the latest work of the star, the movie "Enemy of Women", the story is tightly based on this point, showing the typical figures of two men in society, one is infatuated, the other is a deceiver, and at the same time, the true meaning of love and the dynamic changes are fully developed and severely criticized. May friends who talk about love and say love, go to the fabric of its scenes, to see all the ugly and beautiful grinding of the exposed posture!

Small Knowledge

Prevention and Elimination of the Four Major Pests of Summer 227

— Bingyu

As the summer season arrives, the climate is getting hotter, and various harmful insects will multiply day by day in the future. During this period, we should pay attention to prevention to avoid being harmed by infectious diseases. Among the harmful insects, the most dangerous one is the fly. According to surveys by hygienists, the number of germs in a fly ranges from as few as five hundred and fifty to as many as six million six hundred thousand. The majority of these germs are E. coli from human and animal feces. These bacteria are the source of cholera, dysentery, typhoid fever, and other diseases. Flies like to eat these bacteria very much, often eating their fill, or vomiting them from their mouths, or excreting them from their anuses. Therefore, in summer, the walls, tables, clothes, and utensils in the room, after the flies have stepped on them, the fecal spots left behind, when viewed under a microscope, contain from one thousand to one million germs. Adding the germs brought by the flies' feet, there are at least more than fifteen thousand. If we eat them directly (from fruits and delicacies) or indirectly (using hands to bring them in from utensils), we will get sick. Flies grow very quickly, from egg to adult, in more than half a month. Flies love the color rose, and the most disliked colors are green, purple, and red. If the windows are fitted with glass of red, purple, and green colors, then flies will not be able to tolerate living indoors. Fly-killing drugs include kerosene emulsion, borax, carbon tetrachloride, chloroform (a colorless, transparent, strongly volatile substance with a foul odor and good sterilization properties), ether, gasoline, chloropicrin, etc. However, fly pupae are more resistant to insecticides than maggots. Therefore, using a 10% solution of cresol soap liquid can completely eliminate them in five minutes. Using a 10 to 20 times diluted kerosene emulsion can also kill 80 to 90 percent of them.

Mosquitoes

Mosquitoes are also one of the vectors of infectious diseases. There are two hundred species of mosquitoes. One laying produces at least seventy or eighty eggs and up to three or four hundred eggs. The basic requirements for mosquito control are (1) clear the drainage of sewage ditches, (2) cut down weeds around ponds and rivers, (3) tidy up the cleanliness of wet places, (4) pour kerosene on the water surface to prevent mosquitoes from breeding in the water, (5) if in the room, to prevent them from disturbing at night, camphor, pyrethrum, and duckweed can be mixed and burned in the room, and the mosquitoes will definitely flee.

Fleas

There are human fleas, dog fleas, cat fleas, and rat fleas. To prevent the occurrence of fleas, first, sweep the room clean, and second, often sprinkle with stinky medicine. Dog and cat fleas can be controlled by mixing camphor, pyrethrum, and naphthalene disinfectant and applying it to the fur of dogs and cats or spreading it on the bedding, which can definitely drive them away.

Bedbugs

Bedbugs reach their egg-laying period in the plum rain season. Before laying eggs, special attention should be paid to driving them away. During this period, it is best to use steam disinfection and kerosene spraying in the crevices of partitions, the frame of the bed, and dry, dark places. However, these pests are most common in poor families. Steam disinfection is ultimately not possible, and kerosene spraying poses a fire hazard. According to my experience, it is best to rinse with boiling water, or mix crab shells, spicy eggplants, and papayas in wood shavings, tightly close the doors and windows to prevent leakage, and burn them indoors. This can completely eliminate them, but when burning, this smoke is very strong, and we will feel dizzy when we touch this smoke. Therefore, after burning, be sure to open the doors and windows first, and do not touch this smoke too much. If we want a quiet night on the road, we can add realgar to salt water and spray it on the bed frame.
