Free Talk

Awakening from Illusion 228

— Feixin

Everyone always goes from small to big. The most valuable thing is old age, and the most important thing is youth. Problems that old people don't consider important are big problems for young people. Therefore, youth problems, even if they are considered pitiful and ridiculous, are big problems. All wise people, those who understand, those who have experience and ideas, should provide guidance.

Just as the purpose of fruit is to rot and regrow into better fruit. In the journey of life, everyone is a passerby: like those who visit mountains and rivers, they should point out the best scenic spots to those who come later, and of course point out the dangerous places, or flatten them for those who come.

So many people say: experience is knowledge, which is correct. Apart from life, what is the use of academic knowledge? There is none. Many people read books, but if it has nothing to do with oneself or others, it does not count as knowledge.

But simply imparting experience has both advantages and disadvantages. The motive is commendable, but the selection of skills must be cautious. Ruan Ji's son asked to drink alcohol, but Ruan Ji refused, "My family already has Ah Xian," which is exactly the behavior of a philosopher, which is not to center on oneself and teach the world to learn from oneself.

But looking at old families sometimes educating their children, teaching them to gamble, they want them not to lose; teaching them martial arts, they hope they will not be defeated; teaching them to wander, they want them not to be desolate. The most common thing is to teach them to socialize and hope they will conform to the world. Although it is the intention of the benevolent, it is quite far from the way of education.

That mistake is still because it is centered on oneself. If young people are taken as young people, they have their own development and future. Many situations and environments have changed, and the old methods are useless. This kind of mistake can be avoided.

There is no regret for self-gain and self-loss, the regrettable thing is repeated mistakes; there is not enough sorrow for those who move forward and collapse, the sad thing is treading on the same mistakes. 丨丨 We see the suffering of many young people today, there are conflicts with their families, there are disputes with the opposite sex. In fact, all parties have good intentions, but they get bad results. Who sees the motive? The crux is here.

Therefore, Buddha said to advocate no emotion, and Legalists are strict and have little kindness.

Miscellaneous Notes on Reading "Imperial Ming Dynasty Novels" 229

— Shu

(I)

Everyone knows that in modern novels there is "The Travels of Lao Ts'an." Readers of "The Travels of Lao Ts'an" also know that there is Daming Lake in Jinan, and even more know that there is the Temple of Tie Xuan on Daming Lake, and the tragic death of Tie Xuan. However, no one can tell the tragic situation of Tie Xuan's family after his death. Even Hu Shi, who is as broad as having "the addiction to textual research and history," does not seem to have mentioned it in his research.

Recently, I read Wang Ao's "Zhenze J闻," and there is a passage that involves this matter, saying that after Tie Xuan was killed, "his family members were sent to the Jiaofang as prostitutes. Xuan had two daughters, who both swore not to be humiliated. When Emperor Renzong ascended the throne, he pardoned them, and they both married court officials. The two daughters wrote poems to describe themselves. The elder daughter's poem says:

The Jiaofang's rouge washes away the leaden brilliance,

A peaceful heart faces the falling flowers.

Listening to the old tunes, there is still resentment,

Returning to the old garden, there is no home.

A cloud is half tied before the dressing mirror,

Rain and tears flow in vain, wetting the crimson gauze.

Today I meet Bai Sima,

I retell my pipa story before the wine.

Her younger sister's poem says:

Flesh and blood are wounded and the old business is barren,

How can this body bear to return to prostitution?

Tears fall like jade strings, leaving the official residence,

Stepping on golden lotuses, entering the Jiaofang.

Looking in the mirror, I pity my captivating appearance,

Shamed to learn the makeup of a woman leaning against the door.

Spring brings rain and dew as wide as the sea,

Marrying a Tao Lang is better than a Ruan Lang.

The former of the two poems is better, because it expresses sorrow and resentment, and a sense of unyielding to the officials, which is much superior to her sister's inevitable "spring rain and dew" in terms of personality, and the former is superior to the latter not only in terms of poetic technique. I specially record this to tell the readers of "The Travels of Lao Ts'an."

(II) Since the Yuan brothers of the Ming Dynasty advocated expressing nature and spirit, and clarifying the true meaning of language, there was a lot of debate for a while. Some sympathized with the Public Security School and opposed Li and Wang, some supported Li and Wang and opposed the Public Security School, some did not comment, and some disagreed with both. Chen Yubi belonged to the last group. He said:

"When writing, there is no need to discuss oddity or antiquity, but one must form one's own opinion. Reading it from beginning to end makes sense, without any omissions, then it is a good article, and one can also observe the person's actions, career, and enjoyment. Nowadays, people only seek novelty and plagiarism, without any heartfelt and true views. I compare it to an ordinary person wearing a cloth robe, which is still good clothing. If it is cut and patched with silk and satin, although it is expensive, it is not complete clothing after all. If a poor family eats beans and millet, it is still good food. If a beggar gets wine and meat from the grave, although it is a lot, it is ultimately cheap and shameful." This is seen in Yubi's book "Opinions," showing dissatisfaction with both sides and forming his own third faction. However, comparatively speaking, sympathy for the Public Security School is better than that for Yu Lin and Yuan Mei. The literary situation at that time can be seen from this.

(III) Li Bai of the Tang Dynasty, people only know him as a poet, but do not know that his prose also has the same style as his poems. Gu Yuanqing's " 曝偶谈" once asked Hu Wenmu to transcribe his three posts.

The first one says: "Riding a boat and treading on the moon, in a Westerner's tavern, I unknowingly forget both people and things, and my body is outside the world."

The second one says: "Waking up under the moon at night, the shadows of flowers fall and bid farewell, filling my chest, as if washing my soul in an ice pot."

The third one says: "The building is empty and the moon is white, the autumn sky transforms everything, leaning on the railing here, my life is flying, holding the wine and forgetting myself, where does this carriage go?" Yuanqing said that this post "cannot be said by anyone but Taibai," which can be said to be true.

(IV) Tian Rucheng's "Alleyway Anecdotes" has a legend about the Water Margin, which is very strange. It says, "Luo Guanzhong of Qiantang was a man of the Southern Song Dynasty. He compiled dozens of novels, and the preface to the Water Margin describes the treacherous thefts of Song Jiang and others in great detail. However, the changes and deceptions are endless, corrupting people's minds, and his descendants for three generations were all dumb. Such is the reward of good fortune. "This kind of legend is not known on what it is based. It seems unreliable.

(V) Many people in the Ming Dynasty learned the lifestyle of Su Dongpo. At that time, some people criticized it as "people of this world, nowhere are they not Su." I have recorded it before. Recently, I read Zhang Fengyi's Tan Lu, and I also saw a passage saying that "in recent times, scholars and officials often take a monk with them when they retire from illness, in order to show their loftiness. People see it and say that it is the work of Su Changgong and Foyin." The literary customs at that time can be seen from this. If today the Panchen Lama is able to hold Vajra Dharma meetings in Hangzhou, and is welcomed everywhere from top to bottom, it also has a Su flavor, but its function is even greater than calling oneself lofty.

(VI) Legendary operas flourished in the Yuan and Ming dynasties. Hong Wenke recorded in "Glimpses of the Past and Present," "In the past, heroes and chivalrous men, secret plans and wonderful strategies, were delightful and surprising, and truly illuminated the ages. Taishi Gong recorded them in detail. However, how many people in the world are scholars who wield pens and examine books? How many ordinary men and women are ignorant of them?

Our dynasty's poets and writers wrote about Washing Yarn, Hong Fu, Stealing Talismans, and Throwing Pens, etc., in which there are generous and tragic songs, and elegant and outstanding men who established world-shaking achievements, and chivalrous women with transcendent and great knowledge, composing them into lyrics and operas, performing them on the stage, so that the events of that year are vividly in front of our eyes. All those with blood and energy know to strive for excellence. This is truly a help to stimulate people's hearts, and can be called a grand achievement. If one only regards this as the same as puppets in terms of sound and clothing and laughs at them together, then one is truly a wooden or stone person." Using the perspective of carrying the Tao to discuss the Yuan and Ming operas is certainly not entirely correct, but the reason why the Yuan and Ming operas developed completely due to the reason of popularization, the reason of being easy to understand, can also be seen in this section.

(VII) I have already remembered a lot about the past events of non-resistanceism. However, this kind of material can still be picked up at will. The origin of non-resistanceism in China truly makes people have deep thoughts. Wang Qi's "Miscellaneous Records of Yupu" records one of the events: "Yang, Mr. Zhu, was a compiler, living in the capital. A neighbor lost a chicken and scolded him by his surname. His family members told him, and Mr. Yang said, 'In the market, I am not the only one with the surname Yang.' Also, a neighbor's residence is very narrow, and when it rains, water must flow out from Mr. Yang's house, suffering a lot from its dampness. His family members reported it again, and Mr. Yang explained, 'There are more sunny days than rainy days.' His virtue is like this." According to this, two more non-resistanceists have been added in history.

(VIII) In the notes of the predecessors, there are often small articles full of interest. Written casually, with a few words, they fully express the beauty. I especially like to choose and record them. Wang Shimao's "酉委谭" also has no shortage of such texts, such as:

"On May 12th, I returned from the county town and slept very tired at night. I hated to hear the sound of mosquitoes, and did not sleep for a long time. The street drum was about to move, and I finally fell asleep. Suddenly, the sound of gurgling outside the window made me hope for rain. Lying half awake on a bamboo bed with a cloth quilt, I called the servant girl to beat me, and I listened to it all. I felt that the tired bear was completely revived. Checking my chest, there was nothing at all, only the topic for my son's composition had been given the night before. As I tossed and turned, I heard my old wife calling, probably urging the servants to collect yellow plum water and pick jasmine flowers. She is doing this unnecessary task again, I smiled. I put on my clothes and got up, combed my hair, burned incense, and finished reciting the scriptures. I went out and sat in the Xinyuan Hall, picked up a pen, stretched out the paper, and wrote a few lines to record it."

Talking About Ghosts 230

— Lingmo

Every day, I just flip through the newspaper casually. I can't figure out big things, and I can't take care of small things. But since I'm reading the newspaper, I always want people to think that "the scholar doesn't go out but knows everything in the world." Today, the cook who delivers food asked me again how the ghost in Zhabei was reported in the newspaper. He was preparing to go and see it from afar in the afternoon, so he asked me to collect some reference materials for him. Seeing his enthusiasm, I took a deep breath myself.

Zhang Jiuguan's "Scientific Spirit Planchette Chart" has not yet made people feel that there are too many ghosts, so new spiritual miracles are constantly being created. Although Mr. Zhitang's "Listening to Talk About Ghosts in the Streets All Day Long" has already been scolded a lot, judging from the news in Shanghai, I dare not say that it is not a fact. In the eyes of people in Beijing, Shanghai has long been a paradise, and Shanghai is also unavoidable to see ghosts. It is conceivable that Beijing has long been filled with ghost stories.

In such an economic downturn, there is inevitably a lot of vacant space that cannot be rented out. People in Shanghai, who are used to every inch of land being gold, are not yet used to thinking about why houses cannot be rented out, so they naturally turn to making a fuss about the auspicious character in "auspicious house for rent." In the past, rooms in large restaurants where suicides had occurred would be moved into immediately before the blood stains were dry, but now they may be empty for several months.

Except for winning the lottery, it is now difficult for people to hope for unexpected good luck. No matter what business they are engaged in, they shake their heads when they talk about it, and they fail when they do it. The two words "inauspicious" lie in everyone's heart. No matter how this ghost in Zhabei is proven to be empty, it will still add a dark ghost to every inauspicious home.

Even people who don't believe in ghosts are often moved out of an unfortunate house, and some even move several times a week from here to there. There are too many shadows of all kinds, and it is not necessarily a stupid blessing to attribute them to ghosts.

Snakes and Myths 231

— Shushan

It is clearly the year of the dog this year, but the snake insists on stealing the show.

We only need to look at the recent bizarre news about snakes that has been constantly published in the newspapers of Beijing and Shanghai to know that snakes are indeed蠢然思动.

For example: First, a large snake suddenly appeared on the main road in the southern suburbs of Zhenjiang, about ten feet long, binding a farmer, who died of serious injuries. This is, of course, not losing the nature of the snake as a poisonous insect (see "Central Daily News," June 7). Another example is that in the Vienna Dance Hall in Shanghai, just as it was drunken and gold-obsessed, nine strange snakes were suddenly found, which frightened the male and female dancers, and the whole hall was in an uproar. This is another prank by someone.

The most strange thing is the snake that surrounded and protected the girl in Changzhou, and the snake that crowded the bride's sedan chair in Pudong. The former is: "Shi Dewen, a shipowner in Changzhou, and his wife, Shi, gave birth to a son and a daughter each. Recently, they brought back a three-month-old girl from the northern township, intending to raise her as their son's wife. However, the girl was weak and sick due to lack of milk, and soon died. Shi was cruel and wrapped the girl in a cattail bag and sent her to the mountain tomb at night. The next day, a passerby heard a child crying in the tomb and followed the sound to watch. He only saw a snake more than ten feet long, coiled beside the child, protecting her. Several wild dogs stood beside her, wanting to grab the child but dare not. He was very surprised and reported it to the authorities. When the matter became clear, Shi was arrested, and the girl was sent to the orphanage in the city for support." (See "Fiction Monthly," June issue) This snake can truly be said to be a benevolent and righteous snake, almost comparable to the tiger that nursed Chu Ling Yin Ziwen in the Spring and Autumn period.

The latter is seen in the Shanghai newspapers of June 7, the general idea is: "Cao Quanlin, the son of Cao Yinshan in Pudong, was betrothed to Sister Huang Quanlin, a farmer's daughter, when he was young, and had sexual relations before marriage. The crystallization of love is now five months old, so they are marrying early. At that time, the wedding was extravagant and the officials were all present. However, a huge blue-yellow snake, more than ten feet long, suddenly came head-on to the bride's sedan chair in the Guanyin Hall area west of Zhangjiang shed, and went straight into the sedan chair. The bride was frightened and cried out. When the gong was sounded to drive it away, the snake actually raised half of its body, raised its head and bowed, and hissed as if it were sad. After the snake was driven down, the wedding party hurriedly ordered the sedan chair to be carried away, but after traveling a mile, the snake appeared again in front of them. After driving it away again, they finally welcomed her home and got married." It is not known what the reason for this snake is. Could it be that it also has some opinions on this kind of "early transaction, auspicious opening" new marriage?

These two news items are like re-enacting the stories of the mythological era. That's right, snakes have never been separated from the mythical nature in people's minds, regardless of whether they are insects or gods and monsters.

According to the "Historical Records," the people of ancient times, such as Fu Xi and Nu Wa, were all strange people with snake bodies and human heads. When Yu opened the Dragon Gate, he saw a snake god and taught Yu the method of pacifying the land and water. According to "Shi Yi Ji," this was Emperor Xi. Also, "Zuo Zhuan" said that there were snakes fighting inside and outside the south gate of Zheng, which was called a demon. Secondly, there is the legend of "snake beads" in "Sou Shen Ji." The myths of snakes are truly countless.

In foreign countries, there are also many ancient mythological legends about snakes. The "Genesis" in the "Old Testament" records the situation in which the ancestors of mankind, Eve and Adam, were tempted by snakes to steal and eat the fruit of the tree, which is the most powerful one.

In short, snakes are too naughty. The more people are tempted by it to fall, and then hate it, fear it, but also respect it, the more tricks it will come up with and the more skillful it will become.

Recently, the Chinese have been fascinated by its skillful tricks, and are reversing the times.

Fire (VIII) 232

— Fei'er

At first glance, the flames were burning on the second and third shops on the left. The sirens had already started. The fire was so fierce that it went straight up, almost twenty or thirty feet high, illuminating the sky red. The flames filled the sky. The smell of burning things was in the air, and the sound of things exploding could be heard. The flames were spitting in and out, and the wind was driving them, pushing them from one side to the other. Sometimes things like kerosene tanks were seen thrown high into the sky after an explosion, and then falling down again. The sound of the wind, the sound of the fire, the sound of things exploding, and the cries of all the people and dogs mixed together in the darkness of the night.

At the moment, many coolies and many natives were doing the work of moving goods and fighting the fire, coming and going in confusion and haste. On the riverside, the precious shallow water of the receding tide was transported; in front, water was poured into the flames. As soon as the water was poured, the fire subsided, and then it burned even more vigorously. Brave firefighters were dismantling the house on the third right; but the fire was chasing after it faster with the wind. This made it impossible for the firefighters to do anything, especially in this municipally incomplete village.

Seeing that human power was no use, everyone's faces were covered with earthy colors. The women's cries shook the sky, and the men were dumbfounded. Seeing this foundation that had stood for decades or even hundreds of years being destroyed in this moment: seeing the place where thousands of people's livelihoods were entrusted being destroyed, who would not cry for their own history and life!

Here, I found my friend Zhang Wensheng again. I saw him barefoot, tired and frustrated, his face covered with a layer of muddy gray, lying on a small pile of wreckage like he was seriously ill, dying.

I thought that the prediction in the afternoon was actually fulfilled within this day, no, these few hours; I thought about how I strangely ran tens of thousands of miles from the country to participate in this tragedy. Here, watching my little friend from ten years ago trapped in the disasters of life, fulfilling the situation that he had been fearing day and night in his heart, what words would I use to comfort him?

"Friend, be safe! Nothing else matters, listen to the instructions of heaven!" I swallowed these useless words.

"Yes, it does matter, what's going on?" Then, he hissed. I saw his anger as strong as fire.

We were silent. Under this disaster, there was no other way but to silently pass the sad time.

The wind was still driving the fire, and with the help of the fierce burning medium in the burning shops, the fire was getting more lively and more violent. At this time, in the cold wind of this late night, in my heart, it was terribly lonely and empty! My body was shaking constantly; in this red-hot country, I had never felt so cold.

The sky was gradually getting light, and the morning sun was gradually climbing from the east. As soon as the red glow in the east matched the flames, the fire gradually reduced its intense color.

The sun slowly climbed up from the ground, and as soon as its brilliance appeared, the fire gradually subsided. The wind, showing a low mood, had been blowing all night, and now it was gradually tending to stop. People's sad hearts were expressed on their faces, and this tragic expression was clearly exposed in this bright morning. Looking at the site of the shops on the left, which had become ashes, and on the right, the fire was gradually extinguishing, was it about to be extinguished?

This fire lasted until about nine o'clock in the morning before it was completely extinguished. As soon as it dawned, the Dutch government's county magistrate had rushed from the county government office forty miles away on a small steamboat, and immediately cooperated with the local chief (13) to assign police and soldiers to extinguish the remaining fire that was gradually going out. And they sent many natives to build simple "Atta Cu" in the square to accommodate these fire-stricken refugees. In the morning, many pots of hot porridge were also cooked from the chief's palace to comfort these victims. I enjoyed a bowl of porridge given by the Dutch government in this place tens of thousands of miles away from my country, and I will never forget this in my life.

(Note 13) Before the Nanyang Islands were managed by Europeans, they were originally not unified. They were still in the tribal era, and a small place was governed by a chief. After these places were managed by Europeans, the chieftain system was still preserved, and the colonial government gave them a little bit of minor rights, which they were happy to use to help govern the natives.

Silver and Money Industry Approaching the Summer Festival 235

Interbank Lending Remains Steady

An Additional Quarter Percent for "Hua Tou"

Yesterday's market conditions saw a slight improvement due to the approaching Summer Festival (Dragon Boat Festival) and the increased demand for funds, which was higher than usual. The interbank lending market for foreign currency remained at 8% in both the morning and afternoon sessions, unchanged from the previous two days. Due to wider demand, the "hua tou" (a type of short-term loan) market saw more demand than supply, leading to a rate of 0.25%, an increase of 0.125% from the previous day. This phenomenon has not been seen in months. However, in reality, it is due to the traditional emphasis on the Dragon Boat Festival, resulting in increased spending, rather than a genuine advancement in society's economic capacity. The trading volume of interbank lending bills was over 4.4 million in the morning session for transfers and new transactions and over 200,000 in the afternoon session. Trading in the Small General Association totaled over 300,000. Transactions involving foreign currency collateral loans saw over 900,000 redeemed, over 800,000 issued, and over 400,000 collected in cash. Bank receipts and payments were relatively stable. Securities: Prices Rebound in Chaos 238

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange market unexpectedly entered a state of chaos. Grains: Later Flour Market Has Floating Longs Appear 247

Yesterday's flour market saw an active and positive trend in all months after opening in the morning. Due to foreign wheat quotations, Chicago was slightly up by 0.25 cents, and Canada was up by around 0.2 yuan. Therefore, after the opening price, sentiment was quite brisk. In addition, off-market longs were actively buying, especially in the money industry. For customer groups, the Tianjin group showed no intention, only the Yingkou group had some transactions. Therefore, near-term and long-term contracts were 0.01 or 0.015 yuan better than the previous day. However, when the market opened in the afternoon, due to the Tianjin group drawing on gun carriages for this month, the initial opening was quite good, as high as 0.0725 yuan. However, long-term contracts in various months suddenly saw a sharp drop, with floating longs close to manufacturers, making large sales. Small factories also followed suit. Therefore, from July onwards, prices gradually loosened and fell. According to the current situation, it is under the control of off-market traders, and it is impossible to talk about whether spot sales are active. The true market situation can only be judged after wheat accumulates and flour has no way out. As a result, this month was down by 0.005 yuan, July was down by 0.0125 yuan, August was down by 0.015 yuan, September was down by 0.0125 yuan, October was down by 0.01 yuan, and November was down by 0.0175 yuan.

Yesterday's futures wheat market saw a continued brisk trend in all months after opening in the morning. Due to foreign wheat quotations, Chicago was up by 0.25 cents, and Canada was up by as much as 0.2 yuan. New Broad Beans Arrive in Flocks, Continuing to Fall 251

Silk and Tea: Extra Tidbits from the Suzhou Sericulture Season 252

(Many farmers in Jintan kiln-dry cocoons.) This year, the Jintan Model District, along with government offices and silk merchants, jointly invested in the construction of four new-style cocoon firms, using kiln-drying machines. The old cocoon firms throughout the county did not dare to weigh and purchase cocoons because they suppressed prices. On the second day after the start of weighing and purchasing, the four new cocoon firms were vandalized by farmers, leaving silkworm farmers with nowhere to sell their cocoons. They all used local methods to dry the cocoons themselves and transported them to neighboring counties for sale, or entrusted cocoon firms to kiln-dry them in small batches.

(Cocoon firms in Wuxi have already stopped weighing.) A total of 202 cocoon firms have opened in the four rural areas of Wuxi. Weighing and purchasing began many days ago, but cocoon prices are not high. Improved breed cocoons only fetch an average of 35 yuan. The cost of fresh cocoons and leaves for farmers this season is more than 50 yuan per 100 jin (mulberry leaves cost 3.3-3.4 yuan per dan). Because of losses, it is difficult to sell, and many dry them themselves. Cocoon firms have only collected 20-30 dan in a few days, and all stopped weighing early. A small number of cocoon firms in the southern countryside are still weighing and purchasing.

(Suzhou dry cocoons are continuously transported to Shanghai.) The spring cocoon market in various counties of Suzhou Province is gradually coming to an end. Dry cocoons from various cocoon firms are now being continuously transported to Shanghai. The dry cocoons from Yixing, Jintan, Changshu, Wuxi, and Jiangyin are mostly loaded onto barges and towed by small steamers to Shanghai.

Red and Green Tea Sales are Booming 253

Yesterday, major foreign firms such as British Trading Company, Jardine Matheson, Ewo, and Tongsfoo were heavily purchasing red tea from Qimen, Fuliang, Ningzhou, Wenzhou, and other places, as well as green tea from Tunxi, Shexian, Suian, and other places. Total transactions in red and green tea throughout the city reached six to seven thousand boxes. The briskness of the trading is unprecedented since the new tea came on the market. Regarding the forms of tea, coarse grades of red tea from Wenzhou and Hekou are still the most popular. Upper and middle grades of tea from Qimen and Ningzhou have also become firmer in the market. As for the destination of green tea, except for local grades of Pingshui, which are slightly sluggish, the rest are sold as soon as they arrive. Even the needle-shaped eyebrow green tea, which has been sluggish for a long time, has become more active in its sales.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Talks

Curiosity and the Chinese 254

— Bin Fu

丨Thoughts Inspired by the Haunting in Hua'an Fang丨

These past few days, a hot wind, mixed with "religious ceremonies" and "scientific spirit writing," has just blown over. A "strange event" has once again been "widely publicized" in the city. It is said that a vacant house in Hua'an Fang, Zhabei, is haunted by ghosts. It is said that "many people are gambling in the vacant house at night, and there are sounds of radio, conversations, and mahjong mixed together. But when the door is knocked and people rush in, there is not a single person inside." So, someone describes it with great animation, and someone listens in stunned silence. Someone else exaggerates it even more vividly, and yet another person listens with their hair standing on end... In this way, it spreads from one to two, and from two to three, all over the streets, shops, "consulates," and "offices." So, people sitting in tea houses talk about it with their legs crossed, shop assistants in foreign cloth stores talk about it leaning on the counters, and passengers on trams talk about it while looking at the red characters on the newspapers. As they talk, they are so excited that white foam appears at their mouths, thoroughly enjoying it. Finally, they conclude: "How strange! How strange!" So, they go to Hua'an Fang together, and suddenly the road where Hua'an Fang is located is filled with "cars like flowing water and horses like dragons."

Oh, how grand! Perhaps there are no people in the world who are as enthusiastic about "curiosity" as we Chinese! No, perhaps there are no people in the world whose "curiosity" is as "pure" as ours. Because other people's curiosity can often become the engine of "research" and "exploration," while our Chinese people's "curiosity" is purely about being "curious" and stops there, without any follow-up. If curiosity leads to various troubles, we Chinese people will definitely not get involved. For example, if Hua'an Fang is haunted, it will undoubtedly arouse a strong "curiosity" in our people. They will not hesitate to spend time spreading the word everywhere, and they will go to see it regardless of the distance. Even if they gain nothing, they will still feel that this is a "strange" event, but they will never investigate the reason for the "strangeness." If someone raises questions such as "Why are there ghosts?" and "What are ghosts?" their "curiosity" will immediately decrease. If someone else uses some scientific explanation to refute this "strange story," they will simply turn away, because that would be too "disappointing."

Even the so-called "scientific spirit writing," a few days ago, simply caused a "city-wide sensation." This is something that someone explained scientifically twenty years ago (Chen Daqi, Superstition and Psychology), but unexpectedly it is appearing again today. This is enough to prove how strong the "curiosity" of the Chinese people is. They do not want "truth" to expose the "strange events" they "love," but would rather have "strange events" obliterate all truth. What scientific explanations and psychological research are simply "eyesores" and "nonsense" in the minds of our "curious" Chinese people!

"Curiosity" seems to have a different meaning in China. Other people's "curiosity" can be maintained for a long time, while Chinese people only rely on temporary impulses. "Curiosity" often leads to careful research in others, while in China it is only a casual pastime. Let me give two examples:

A maid in the home of a certain British aristocrat fell ill one night. During her illness, she suddenly spoke in Greek. Everyone said she was possessed by a demon, because the maid had never learned Greek. When this news spread, many curious people came to visit, which aroused enthusiastic research by psychologists, doctors, detectives, etc. After five or six years, it was finally discovered that the woman had worked as a helper in the home of a linguistics professor, and the linguistics professor read Greek every night. This proved that although the maid had never studied Greek, her subconscious mind had learned it, and it was expressed when her consciousness was blurred and her subconscious mind took over.

If China encountered such a problem, I think it would definitely become an immortal "strange event" and never get such a rational explanation.

What is the "curiosity" of the Chinese people like? The following joke describes it best:

A person was walking down the street and suddenly thought of something. He leaned against a tree on the side of the road and looked up in contemplation. After

Page 20

a while, he suddenly found that he was surrounded by a large circle of people, all looking up and staring. He was shocked and slipped out of the encirclement. When he walked far away, he looked back and saw that more and more people had gathered there, all looking up at the sky where he had been looking, as if searching for something.

Although this is a joke, it is true. Our people are often so idle and curious.

"Curiosity" is originally the driving force of invention, but it needs to go hand in hand with a "love of learning." Most of our people are simply "curious" and not "studious." Although some people say that idleness and curiosity are the demeanor of a great nation, I say that this "unstudious" "curiosity" is the most unprogressive bad habit of our nation!

Written After Reading "How to Control Women" 255

— Xu Bu

After reading Hong Benjun's work, I feel some lingering thoughts. If it is said that women can be controlled, then why can't men be controlled? If everyone rises up to study the art of control in the future, and two sides are clearly formed in opposition, then what is there to say about love? Wouldn't life be even more mechanical? Moreover, in Hongjun's work, women are regarded as puppets. Perhaps Hongjun was momentarily stimulated and rashly wrote this grand article insulting women. Seeing injustice on the road, others are silent, and Xu Bu has no choice but to stand up and write a few words.

Originally, in today's society, there are too many people who do not understand love. Therefore, since the prevalence of free love, many real tragedies have occurred due to the general misunderstanding of love. Both men and women should be equally responsible for this. We should not doubt that all women are like this because of this, and we should not doubt that the true meaning of love is also like this, and say that the sanctity of love is nonsense. It's just that there are too many men and women in the world who despise love like Hongjun, so tragedies of using love to deceive and control people often occur. Perhaps in Hongjun's opinion, it is a ridiculous farce. Seeing love as a purely material matter and wanting to obtain it by tricks is Hongjun's big mistake. Although perhaps the general concept is as Hongjun said, how can it be said that the entire female world is like this!

In my opinion, the two sides of love should understand and care for each other. If it is said that because I love you, I restrict you, that is the biggest mistake in today's discussions about love; it is also a major reason for causing the other party's resentment. Therefore, I think it is better not to be in love before both sides fully understand the true meaning of love. Otherwise, the result will still be a tragedy, and needless to say, a happy family is forever hopeless.

Speaking of women, there are indeed many like Hongjun said, but there are also many who do not follow the crowd. Needless to say, most of the women in the countryside still have sincere love; and even among the women in the flashy city, there are many who are not as Hongjun said. For example, Hongjun said: Women like men to condescend to them, that's right! A portion of women do have this kind of thinking, but how many women will love you because you condescend to them? Isn't it just that men deliberately use their status to lure women? Such men cannot talk about love at all. But generally, pitiful women can indeed fall into the traps of men due to vanity. This is indeed a weakness of general women; but it is not a common weakness of the female world.

Third point: Hongjun said that men's psychology should not be understood by women. Once it is understood, she will attack you, force you, etc. Originally, such a union of men and women has no love in it at all, and there is no need to argue about it. But Hongjun's words do have some points that make people have to say something. These few sentences are not entirely without reason, but these kinds of words can only be said of general women who sell their smiles and have been trained to wink and flirt; and cannot criticize the entire female world.

Again, Hongjun said that women love money. As long as you have money, no matter what kind of man you are, she will stay with you overnight "play the clapper". From this, we can see that Hongjun has only encountered a kind of money-worshipping woman who sells her smiles. He has never seen a truly dignified woman. In Hongjun's view, women are simply playthings, things without souls. Here, he reveals the ugly true face of humanity; forgetting the position of the writer. There are many places that are completely scolding and cannot be described in detail. Only the above few examples can show that the women Hongjun is talking about are all harlots who sell their smiles. It is so boring and ridiculous to use harlots who sell their smiles to compare to the face of the female world.

Now, I have finished speaking. Finally, I advise Hongjun: Women are just like men, both good and bad are mixed together. You cannot criticize the entire female world based on one-sided observations. If you have not deeply observed the specific face, it is better to keep silent to save trouble.

Record of Spiritual Torture 256

— Wen Hei

When I first moved to this new residence, I was very satisfied and happy. The new house in the new alley was called a pavilion room, but it was a pavilion room separated from the front building by a bathroom. In terms of area, it was even larger than the previous front building, and in front of the window was the garden of a rich man's villa. The grass and trees in the garden were lush, and flowers protruded beyond the wall. There was also a hexagonal pavilion. Because the room was large, I lived with Qing, who were both writers. Our temperaments and habits were similar, and we were truly happy. Unexpectedly, one night, one of the people in the front building (who also lived with another man), when I was in bed reading a book and about to sleep, one of them opened the bathroom door and came into our room. I didn't know what he wanted to do and wanted to ask him, but he said to me first, "Did anyone pass through this bathroom at six o'clock last night?" This question was strange! He also said, "We went out to eat at six o'clock, and when we came back, a pair of Chinese silk pants were missing!" I remembered that it seemed that the landlord downstairs was taking a bath last night, and the landlord's wife passed through our room to deliver clothes, so I told him what I remembered. He said, "Someone was taking a bath, no wonder!" He said, returning to his room. Qing was already asleep and probably heard it. He said, "The window there leads to the outside stairwell, I'm afraid they went in through the window." I immediately remembered that the landlord took a bath the day before yesterday, and yesterday I went out in the afternoon and didn't come home until midnight. I didn't know anything, so wasn't what I just said accusing the landlord of theft? Feeling wrong, I lifted the covers from the bed and ran to the front building without even putting on my coat. I said to the man, "The landlord took a bath the day before yesterday, and I wasn't home yesterday and don't know anything." Looking up, I saw the student from the clothing shop downstairs standing there. I also remembered that the student often ran to open his room door during the day, so I told him about it. Turning around, I also told him that the bathroom window leads to the stairwell. The student and him were arguing, and I returned to our room. In bed, I remembered mentioning the student just now, wasn't that also accusing him? I immediately felt that my nerves were messed up tonight. At the same time, I also remembered that the man in the front building came over to me about this matter, wasn't he suspecting that we might have stolen something? Another layer of insulted anger was added to my spirit. I thought of Qing, my roommate... Could it be that he... I can't think about it.

From that night on, my spirit was being tortured.

A few days later, I came home from outside, and when I looked up at the black sign at the entrance of the alley, I saw a red piece of paper with a house for rent, "Front Building No. 2 for Rent." These six words were like a sharp blade stabbing into my heart! They are moving out, they are moving out! Oh my God, they suspect that I, a wanderer in this pavilion room, am a thief! This morning, I was washing my face in the bathroom, and the man in the front building said to me, "The landlord is going to return your room, right?" I said, "No!" He said, "We are moving today!" Oh my God, he has been suspecting me and hating me all along, and he has already told the landlord to return my room! And the landlord must also be suspecting that I, a wanderer, am a thief!

I can't live in this room anymore! Even if the landlord doesn't dismiss us, I can't stand the spiritual torture!

Chinese Women's Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition: Works by the Three Heroes of the Dust 257

— Written by Yu Jing

A More Meaningful Thing 258

— Nan Ding

After three years of cohabitation, I have tasted enough of the taste of "love."

The so-called "happiness of love" is just an illusion.

Economic oppression and social crises have deeply broken into everyone's "territory."

In the beginning, when I began to enter the "love net," everything reflected in my eyes was lively, fresh, and harmonious. However, after three years of life, everything was the opposite of before. We often quarreled and fought over small things, like enemies, without the previous situation of mutual humility. In this way, the surroundings I came into contact with now seemed to have lost their freshness and harmonious existence in my eyes.

From these days on, we were both very clear about each other's actions. Due to inner sensitivity, when I sat down, I knew what she was going to say, and when I lay down, she understood what kind of words I was going to say.

She was tired of everything. She was often annoyed, and often quietly lay on the bed crying alone. Because she always liked me to stay at home and accompany her, but I couldn't do that. Is it that after a person becomes a "home," they have to become a tool, a decoration of the "home"? Or that a person becomes a "lover," becomes a "husband and wife," he or she must become his or her slave?

This is absolutely impossible.

"Marriage is the tomb of love," this sentence has its considerable value. I feel that the so-called "love" is a pastime for the leisure class, especially the pastime of the petty bourgeoisie.

After all, it is distressing, and thinking about it later, I felt even more pain.

So, I often quietly ran to the suburbs alone. In the open and fresh fields, I wandered on that vast land, admiring the green mountains and green waters, trees, flowers, flying birds and running animals, and the beauty of nature, bringing me into a secluded and pure realm. I couldn't help sighing at the good fortune of individual free life.

However, this temporary physical sense of ease, when I returned to my dull "home," was scattered by the east wind like a colorful cloud.

Life is a burden to me, and I understand that this is unavoidable. I am no longer a child of childhood.

Work is a mission to me, and I clearly understand that this is a necessary obligation for me to life; I am no longer just myself.

"I must change, I must change the form of my life!" As I stepped into the "home" door, looking at my wife, who was frowning and waiting for me to come home, I deeply sighed.

She glanced at me, which seemed to be blaming me for leaving her alone in this cold and empty house.

I ignored her and lazily lay on the bed. Looking at the ceiling, looking at this empty and dull little house, thinking about this life, I couldn't help but shudder and then silently thought:

"Love" is hatred to me!

"Life" is disgust to me!

However, I have to live, and she has to love. We are living and loving. Aren't people animals rich in emotion?

However, we are very distressed after all. In love of poverty and depression, aren't we struggling? After three years of love, I have tasted the bitterness of love. I have no love, I cannot love; I hate love! At this time, I feel that there is something more important, more urgent, and more meaningful than love.

Regarding Theater Reviews 259

In the past half month, drama has suddenly become active, which is naturally a very good phenomenon. Moreover, readers have enthusiastically written reviews. But to be honest, the editor is a layman in drama and does not know the situation of the performances. Of course, the value of the drama cannot be estimated in the organization of the text of the submitted drama reviews. Therefore, what is published here are all specially commissioned contributors of this newspaper. At the same time, the writers of theater reviews should bear some responsibility for the text. In the future, I hope that readers will not submit this kind of manuscript. Those who have attached sufficient postage have been returned. I apologize for not answering each inquiry letter individually.

Philosophical Exhaustion 260

— Zi Wu

Innocent children will never think about the matter of life, and old people are unwilling to ask questions about life again: What exactly is it for? Only young people and adults, drilling into this stuffy gourd, try their best to get out. Sometimes they live quietly and peacefully, and sometimes they stir up and shout, "What exactly is life for?" At this time, it should be an extremely depressed moment.

When there are many times of depression, the depths of the heart will never be peaceful.

Moral views of life and religious views of life have long been unable to arouse their life force and cannot hold back their fantasies. They pray for a united life, and at the same time want to develop their own personal personality; they doubt this era and this society, but dare not be sure that they have the ability to transform; they eagerly seek to fulfill real life, and at the same time they recall and envy the past. In a word, they are not satisfied with their current life, but they don't know how to improve it.

For example, socialism is too cold, individualism is too laissez-faire; if the realistic view of life is adopted, life is fundamentally doubted; if the natural view of life is adopted, they are unwilling to be lonely: again, if the so-called true love view of life, and the truth view of life are adopted, then some of the slightest true love and truth cannot be found in this world.

They want everything, and at the same time they don't want anything. What they want is the past and the future, and what they don't want is only what belongs to the present. So, what do they have now?

Stirring, stirring, the depression is intensified, and the stuffy gourd of life still has not been broken from the inside. Finally, doubt, resentment, and disillusionment push people onto a path of decline.

A friend once said to me that if you want to know "what life is for," you only need to commit suicide, but where can these words be said?

Life, life, philosophy's explanation for modern youth has been exhausted and cannot be used at all.

Lawyers' Extra Income 261

— Yafei

"Living in Shanghai is not easy." This saying is most accurate, I think. However, this is certainly not a problem for those living in Western-style houses; but for the average small citizen, the working class, and salaried people, it is indeed a bit frightening! Because the expenditure on rent alone accounts for at least a third of a family's total expenses. Take myself, for example! Living in a small attic room with inconvenient transportation and poor air quality costs me seven dollars a month. Seven dollars is a third of my total monthly income. The remaining two-thirds must cover food, clothing, socializing, medicine, and all other miscellaneous items, so I am constantly broke.

Seven dollars a month, twelve months a year, adds up to eighty-four dollars. Eighty-four dollars could perhaps buy one or two acres of land in the countryside. However, in Shanghai, it can only rent a place the size of a tofu square; with a bed and a small table inside, there is no place to put anything else. Therefore, I often hate urban life and long to live in the countryside, but life tells me; it is impossible, impossible.

Not long ago, someone, seeing that rents were increasing daily and that the general public and shops would have unbearable burdens, and that the future of Shanghai was in decline, initiated a "Rent Reduction Movement Committee" to revive Shanghai's market and prosper the city's commerce. For a time, it rose like a storm, with voices echoing from front to back, and various districts and neighborhoods followed suit; seemingly, the wave of rent reduction

Page 22

Page 23

shook the entire Shanghai. However, it was only a flash in the pan. Nevertheless, this gave several big lawyers a large batch of extra business. Smart lawyers, of course, would not let this opportunity pass, and they printed a large number of warning letters and rent reminder letter formats; when needed, they only needed to fill in the names of the parties, the amount of rent, and the recipient, as it was all the same monotonous article.

The court also added an unknown number of civil lawsuits for rent arrears.

Originally, money can communicate with gods, and the landlords naturally wouldn't keep these ant-like tenants in mind.

Speaking of their countermeasures, there are no more than three methods: First, if the tenant insists on reducing the rent and refuses to pay without a reduction, then they simply don't come to collect it. After a considerable period, they request legal assistance to collect the owed rent, not fearing that you will be shortchanged by a single cent. The second is to use harsh measures of cutting off water and transportation to pressure the tenants. Both water and transportation are necessities that cannot be lacking for even a moment in daily life. By monopolizing the source of these two things, they are not afraid that you will not compromise with them. When the compromise is reached, they will have a victorious smile. The third is the last resort, selling or mortgaging the original property, allowing the new owner to declare renovation and force relocation. There are also a few unscrupulous landlords who even use the name of foreign merchants to oppress tenants.

On the other hand, in today's declining countryside, whole batches of villagers are dreaming of a golden city and flowing into the city, thus causing inevitable and uncoordinated conflicts in urban society's consumption and production. The investment eyes of the financial and banking sectors, however, avoid commercial and industrial enterprises and lean towards the real estate industry, causing Shanghai's market to develop in an unbalanced and deformed way. The increase in real estate prices and rents is an inevitable fact. Although, recently, due to the initiation of the Rent Reduction Movement, and further promoted by the Citizens' Federation, citizens in various districts and neighborhoods have continued to organize rent reduction branches, the rent reduction movement continues to make noise day by day. In the end, it still cannot alleviate the burden on the citizens by even a penny, and the disputes are expanding day by day, and the housing problem remains unsolved. Because the law will never help tenants because of the market downturn, rent arrears must of course be repaid, and if they are not, the door will inevitably be sealed.

Wound 262

— Wenlan

Born without a hometown.

All over the world, he wanders, ceaselessly and forever wandering, from here to there.

It was also by chance! He stayed with us.

Wearing a tattered coat obtained from who knows where, a bamboo pole always carried with him, barefoot, from as far back as he can remember, he recognizes that he has never changed. He has lived for more than twenty years, he has not accumulated a single penny, his life is one of shouting with his mouth every day. However, this mouth of his is not clever, because he knows too little about "speaking nicely." This not-so-clever mouth of his really makes him suffer, often not getting any rice or porridge, only receiving a cold face. When he meets a cranky person, he gets a scolding head-on. He endures all this. He is hungry and has no choice but to beg from door to door.

The psychology of wanting to improve once moved him, "Isn't he just a young man in his early twenties? He has strength and should find a proper life," but the following difficulty made him feel dull again. Where to go in today's declining industries? And who can accommodate him, a beggar?

Yet he lives, shouting with his mouth every day.

He is not as well-off as other beggars, he knows how much he hates this not-so-clever mouth!

At the corner of the alley, he frantically sings out-of-tune songs. Then, a group of children gather around, pointing at him and saying, "Crazy beggar."

When he feels intense pain, he sings, sobbing in the cold weather, the wind carrying such mournful and sorrowful tunes.

He wants to live, he has to live, but his means of seeking life are incompetent. Once, walking past a place full of people's clothes drying, this white cluster of clothes clearly shook his thoughts on how to seek life. Before his eyes, this opportunity, easy, profitable, and wonderful, could satisfy his desires for a few days. He hesitated, and finally pulled down a silk dress and turned to prepare to run. Suddenly, a person chased after him from that doorway, and vaguely he felt a door bolt as thick as a pillar strike him in the waist, "Thief! You thief!" such a stern shout.

Now, he will not come out to beg, never again come out to beg for the few leftovers exchanged for the endless beatings and scoldings of cruel humanity. He lies prostrate at the entrance of an ancient temple, on that loose pile of straw, caressing the wound he received for wanting to satisfy a little of life. He thinks of home, thinks of his mother, he weeps, not daring to cry aloud, he sobs softly.

Going to the City 263

— Rongxi

Dad is going to the city! Speaking of the city, Little Silly couldn't help but feel envious again!

He remembers that the city has four-wheeled cars, horse carriages, and revolving colored lights at the entrances of shops... there are so many things! Really, Little Silly wishes he could live there forever!

In the evening, Dad came home. Little Silly's eyes were fixed on Dad's face. Dad's face didn't have the usual smile, it was always gloomy! Iron-blue.

For the past two months, Dad hasn't gone to the factory, he has been pacing the streets every day. He also doesn't bring back tasty things in his hands when he comes home, like he used to. Little Silly would take them and put them in his little basket, Dad would stroke his black hair, and a gentle and loving smile would appear on his face. But now it's different! When Little Silly sees his father coming home, he will retreat a few steps in fear!

At this time, Mom stares at Dad, and Little Silly also stares at Dad. Dad always hangs his head, and the room is strangely desolate!

"How is it..."

Mom said, trembling.

Dad didn't make a sound, just shook his head.

Little Silly felt strange, Dad was really like a robber seeing an official, wasn't Dad always talking and laughing before?!

"Mom, who made Dad angry?"

Mom was like Dad, not making a sound. Mom's eyes were shining. Little Silly never got the answer to this mystery.

"When a person loses their job, all hope is really gone."

Mom sobbed.

Little Silly didn't believe that such a good person like Dad would have nothing to do! Dad doesn't go out to play with women, doesn't smoke, doesn't gamble. Really, he believes that Dad is a good person without any flaws! Mom's lips trembled again, still so trembling:

"Why don't we go to the city and borrow some from uncle." Little Silly was excited again when he heard about going to the city. Dad had said many times about going to the city, but it never happened. He looked at Dad suspiciously.

"There's no way, Mom, it's so hard to find a job through someone! I'm afraid borrowing will be in vain..."

Dad was obviously angry, and Little Silly became a little scared. However, hope finally overcame fear. He asked:

"Mom, Mom, I want to go."

Mom didn't express anything, Mom only said faintly:

"Mom isn't going, you shouldn't go either."

After a pause, Mom continued:

"Dad doesn't have much money now, we'll take you when he has a job later."

Little Silly's enthusiasm suddenly disappeared. Only a trace of fear remained! Looking at Dad's iron-blue face, he didn't have the courage to say he wanted to go again.

Early in the morning, Little Silly got up. Dad ate a few Henan pancakes, put them in the bag on his back, and was about to leave when Mom said:

"Tell him about our hardships."

Dad nodded, put on his broken felt hat and left. "Mom, is Dad going to borrow money from uncle?"

Mom's hardworking hand stroked Little Silly's hair, Little Silly felt all kinds of tenderness, Mom stared blankly at Dad's back, tears falling down, Mom was stunned.

Travel Notes

Impressions of Chang'an (5) 264

— Yunshan

8. Southerners in Chang'an

"Go to the Northwest!"

The loudness and novelty of this call were no less than the revolutionary fervor of "Go to the People!" and "Go to the Countryside!" during the Northern Expedition era.

I really went to the "Northwest." And I saw many southerners who had already arrived and were "living and working in peace!" Among them, naturally, there are many small industrialists and merchants who have lived here for a long time and have almost assimilated with the local area. There are also many who have become noble due to political changes.

Occasionally passing through the streets and alleys, hearing a few soft Wu dialects, I, a lonely traveler in this foreign land, really felt the joy of "meeting an old acquaintance in a foreign land!" But upon closer inspection: no way! People have such a luxurious and dignified air, how can you, this little nobody, squeeze in? In the end, I still felt ashamed of myself, spat, and walked away!

Horseback riding in the suburbs should have a special flavor around this ancient city, but I didn't have the opportunity to really experience it. During this time of the Yangchun March, when the scenery in the north is still good, every time in the slanting sunset, I see two or three young girls, 丨丨 of course also from the south! Lightly dressed and lightly made up, flaunting on tall steeds. Using a Chengyu from the Liaozhai: "Passersby looked back and followed them with their eyes." Afterwards, there are always a few unimportant idle comments:

"Our southern women are still beautiful! Look: how beautiful she is riding on a horse!" The southerners who opened small shops evoked memories of the spring scenery of Jiangnan.

"Rare? That's just the old trick of 'the wife gains glory from the husband's success!'" Another merchant said angrily:

"I don't know whose concubine this is? Their good fortune is so great...!" The coolies on the road sighed to themselves that they were not as good!

9. The Important People Inspecting the Northwest

The important people's inspection of the Northwest is either for the construction of the accompanying capital, or for the development of the countryside; or perhaps due to the emotion of drinking water and thinking of the source, they specially ran back to their "old home" to visit the graves. (The Northwest is the old home of the Han people in history.)

Regarding the construction of the accompanying capital, I saw that there was already a wooden sign for the "Preparatory Committee of Western Capital," and I don't know how long it had been established. Regarding returning to the "old home" to visit the graves, there are many examples, too numerous to list. Only the construction of rural development, because the project of the Tongxi section of the Longhai Railway has already been concretely carried out, does indeed show some new atmosphere.

First, the landlords of Chang'an have built countless earthen enclosures on the abandoned wasteland inside and outside the city to show where the sovereignty lies. Their greatest hope is that after the railway is opened, land prices will rise and they can make a fortune!

Second, the hotel industry is booming, and a magnificent building has been newly built across from the Xijing Hotel on Dongda Street. In the future, its business will be more developed than the current Northwest Hotel.

Third, the Yuqin Textile Company, which is preparing in Sanyuan, and the National Northwest College of Agriculture and Forestry, which is being built in Wugong, are closely related to the livelihood of the Northwest people.

Fourth, the power of the great powers will, with the development of inland transportation in China, penetrate deeper into the bottom layer of the rural Northwest, reaching everywhere!

In short, "The Dao is one foot high, and the Devil is ten feet high!" Everything is relative. To develop the Northwest, internally, we must pay attention to the actual benefits to the common people. Externally, we must prevent the disasters that the great powers will bring in the future.

"Beware of peeling and plundering!" I would like to give these four words to those who are truly responsible! 丨丨丨End丨丨丨
